<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
	$('img[name="imgRecentProduct"]').each(function() {
		var imgUrl = $(this).attr('data-src');
		$('img#imgRecentProduct' + i).attr('src', imgUrl).load(function() {
		}).error(function() {
			$(this).attr('src', ctx + '/assets/desktop/img/alfacart_default.png');
		});
		i++;
	});
});
var url = ctx + "/shoppinglist/dashboard";
var ul = $("#ul");
var cats;

if(getCookie("tbtcTotal") != null){
	$("#totalcart").html(getCookie("tbtcTotal"));
}

$("#shopppingListHeader").click(function(){
	$.ajax({
		type : 'GET',
		url  : "/shoppinglist/dashboard",
		datatype : 'json',
		cache: 'false',
		success: function(data){
			ul.empty();
			ul.append('<div class="col-xs-12 shoppinglist-header">'+
			'<p>Shopping List<span class="shoppinglist-count">'+data.totalRows+'</span></p></div>');
			$.each(data.listShopping, function(i,v){
				var totalitem = v.totalitem == null ? 0: parseInt(v.totalitem,10);
				var subtotal = v.subtotal == null ? 0:parseInt(v.subtotal,10);
				ul.append('<li>'+
				'<div class="col-xs-12 sl-hm-list">'+
					'<p class="sl-hm-hdr no-margin">'+v.listname+'</p>'+
					'<div class="col-xs-6 sl-mn-wrapper-left">'+
						'<p>Jumlah Barang</p>'+
						'<p>TOTAL</p>'+
						'<a href="/shoppinglist/'+v.listid+'" class="btn">Lihat Rincian <i class="fa fa-angle-right"></i></a>'+
					'</div>'+
					'<div class="col-xs-6 sl-mn-wrapper-right">'+
						'<p>'+totalitem+'</p>'+
						'<p><span>Rp '+currencyFormat(subtotal)+'</span></p>'+
						'<a href="' + ctx + '/addtocartshoppinglist/' + v.listid + '" class="btn">Add to Cart</a>'+
					'</div>'+
				'</div>'+
			'</li>');
			});
			ul.append('<div class="col-xs-12 shoppinglist-footer text-center">'+
			'<a href="/shoppinglist" class="btn btn-shoplist-all">lihat semua shopping list</a>'+
			'</div>');
		}
	});
});

function getCookie(name){
  var re = new RegExp(name + "=([^;]+)");
  var value = re.exec(document.cookie);
  return (value != null) ? unescape(value[1]) : null;
}

function fetchJSONFile(path, callback) {
    var httpRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
    httpRequest.onreadystatechange = function() {
        if (httpRequest.readyState === 4) {
            if (httpRequest.status === 200) {
                var data = JSON.parse(httpRequest.responseText);
                if (callback) callback(data);
            }
        }
    };
    httpRequest.open('GET', path);
    httpRequest.send(); 
};

function setCategories(item, index) {
	var span = '<span><img id="cat'+item.id+'" src="'+item.icon+'" /></span>' + item.name;
	var menu = 	$('<li>', {class: 'dropdown-submenu dropdown2'}).append(
					$('<a>', {href: item.url, class: 'opensub'}).html(span)
				);
	if (item.subCategory.length > 0) {
		var subCat = $('<ul>', {class: 'dropdown-menu category-floor category-floor-sub dropdown2-2'});
		item.subCategory.forEach(function(item, index){
			setSubCategory(subCat, item, index);
		});
		menu.append(subCat);
	}
	menu.hover(function(){
// 		$(this).children().next('ul.dropdown2-2').toggle();
		$('#cat'+item.id).attr('src', item.iconHover);
	}, function(){
// 		$(this).children().next('ul.dropdown2-2').toggle();
		$('#cat'+item.id).attr('src', item.icon);
	})	
	
	$('#catNavbar').append(menu);
}

// function setBanner(div, item, index) {
// 	div.append($('<img>', {src: item.url}));
// }

function setSubCategory(main, item, index) {
	var menu = 	$('<li>', {class: 'dropdown-submenu dropdown3'}).append(
					$('<a>', {href: item.url, class: 'opensub'}).text(item.name)
				);
	var subDiv = $('<div>', {class: 'col-xs-6 thirdsub-banner'});
	var subCatUl = $('<ul>', {class: 'dropdown-menu category-floor category-floor-sub category-floor-subsub dropdown3-3'});
	var subCat = $('<div>', {class: 'col-xs-6 thirdsub'});		
	item.subCategory.forEach(function(item, index){
		setSubCategory2(subCat, item, index);
	});
	subDiv.append(
			$("<a>", {
			    href: "#", 
			    class: "img-href-1",
			    html: $('<img>', {src:  ctx + '/assets/desktop/img/alfacart_default.png', class: 'thirdsub-img-banner img-0'})
			})
	);
	subDiv.append(
			$("<a>", {
			    href: "#",
			    class: "img-href-2",
			    html: $('<img>', {src:  ctx + '/assets/desktop/img/alfacart_default.png', class: 'thirdsub-img-banner img-1'})
			})
	);
	
	subCatUl.append(subCat);
	subCatUl.append(subDiv);
	menu.append(subCatUl);
	
// 	item.banner.forEach(function(item, index){
// 		setBanner(subDiv, item, index);
// 	});
	
	main.append(menu);
}

function setSubCategory2(main, item, index) {
	var menu = 	$('<li>', {class: 'dropdown-subsubmenu'}).append(
					$('<a>', {href: item.url, class: 'opensub'}).text(item.name)
				);
	main.append(menu);
}


$(document).ready(function(){
	fetchJSONFile('/getCategories', function(data){
	    window.cats = data;
		data.categories.forEach(setCategories);
		window.cur_cat = -1;
		window.cur_subcat = -1;
		$('ul.nav li.dropdown2').hover(function() {
				window.cur_cat = $(this).index();
				$(this).find('ul.dropdown2-2:first').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeIn(10);
				$(this).find('ul.dropdown3-3:first').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeIn(10);
				if (cats.categories[cur_cat].banner.length > 0) {
					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0').attr('src', cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[0].url);
					if (cats.categories[cur_cat].banner.length > 1) {
						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1').attr('src', cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[1].url);
					} else {
						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1').attr('src', '');
					}
				} else {
					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0:first').attr('src', '');
					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', '');
				}
		}, function() {
				window.cur_cat = -1;
				$(this).find('ul.dropdown2-2:first').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeOut(10);
				$(this).find('ul.dropdown3-3:first').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeOut(10);
		});
		
		$('ul.dropdown2-2 li.dropdown3').hover(function(){
				window.cur_subcat = $(this).index();
				$(this).find('ul.dropdown3-3:first').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeIn(10);
// 				if (cats.categories[cur_cat].subCategory[cur_subcat].banner.length > 0) {
// 					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0:first').attr('src', cats.categories[cur_cat].subCategory[cur_subcat].banner[0].url);
// 					if (cats.categories[cur_cat].subCategory[cur_subcat].banner.length > 1) {
// 						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', cats.categories[cur_cat].subCategory[cur_subcat].banner[1].url);
// 					} else {
// 						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', '');
// 					}
// 				} else {
// 					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0:first').attr('src', '');
// 					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', '');
// 				}
				if (cats.categories[cur_cat].banner.length > 0) {
					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0').attr('src', cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[0].url);
					if (cats.categories[cur_cat].banner.length > 1) {
						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1').attr('src',  cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[1].url);
						$(this).find('.img-href-1').attr('href', cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[0].target);
						$(this).find('.img-href-2').attr('href', cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[1].target);
					} else {
						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1').attr('src', '');
					}
				} else {
					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0:first').attr('src', '');
					$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', '');
				}
		}, function(){
				if ($(this).index() > 0) {
					$(this).find('ul.dropdown3-3:first').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeOut(10);
				} else {
					if (cats.categories[cur_cat].banner.length > 0) {
						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0:first').attr('src', cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[0].url);
						if (cats.categories[cur_cat].banner.length > 1) {
							$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', cats.categories[cur_cat].banner[1].url);
						} else {
							$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', '');
						}
					} else {
						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-0:first').attr('src', '');
						$(this).find('.thirdsub-banner .img-1:first').attr('src', '');
					}
				}
				window.cur_subcat = -1;
		});
		$('.dropdown1').on({
			"shown.bs.dropdown": function() { this.closable = false; },
			"click":             function() { this.closable = true; },
			"hide.bs.dropdown":  function() { return this.closable; }
		});
		$('ul.nav li').hover(function() {
			var $this = $(this);
			if ($this.hasClass("keep-open")) {
				$('ul.dropdown1-1').hover(function() {
					$('.dimmed').css('display','block');
				}, function() {
					$('.dimmed').css('display','none');
				});
		    }
		    if ($this.hasClass("open")) {
				$('ul.dropdown1-1').hover(function() {
					$('.dimmed').css('display','block');
				}, function() {
					$('.dimmed').css('display','block');
				});
		    }
		});
		
		$('ul.nav li.dropdown-pst-info').hover(function() {
			$(this).find('.pst-info').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeIn(10);
		}, function() {
			$(this).find('.pst-info').stop(true, true).delay(1).fadeOut(10);
		});
	});
});

<script type="text/javascript">
	var ctx = "";
	var sellerRegist = "https://sofia.alfacart.com/login";
	
	function login() {
		var currentPath = document.URL;
		currentPath = currentPath.replace(document.location.origin +'/fo/', '');
		currentPath = currentPath.replace(document.location.origin +'/', '');
		//alert(currentPath);
		var url;
		if(currentPath == ''){
			url = ctx + '/login?return=';
		}else{
			url = ctx + '/login?return=' + currentPath;
		}
		window.location.href = url;
	}

var floorJSON;

var curDate = new Date();

function set_countdown(element, endDate) {
		setInterval(function time(){
			  var d = new Date(endDate) - new Date(); 
			  var days = 0;
			  var hours = Math.floor((d / (1000 * 60 * 60)));
			  var min = Math.floor((d / (1000 * 60)) % 60);
			  if((min + '').length == 1){
			    min = '0' + min;
			  }
			  var sec = Math.floor((d / 1000) % 60);
			  if((sec + '').length == 1){
			        sec = '0' + sec;
			  }
			  if (days > 1)
				  jQuery(element).html(days + 'd ' + hours + ' : ' + min + ' : ' + sec);
			  else if(d > 0)
				  jQuery(element).html(hours + ' : ' + min + ' : ' + sec);
			  else
				  jQuery(element).html('');
			}, 1000);
}

$(".home-floor-icon").mouseover(function(){
	var bgColor = $(this).data('color');
	var bgHover = $(this).data('hoverin');
	var index = $(this).data('index');
	$(".floor-icon" + index).css('background-color', bgColor);
	$("#imgIcon" + index).attr('src', bgHover);
});

$(".home-floor-icon").mouseout(function(){
	var bgHover = $(this).data('hoverout');
	var index = $(this).data('index');
	$(".floor-icon" + index).css('background-color', 'transparent');
	$("#imgIcon" + index).attr('src', bgHover);
});

			data : 'listName='+listName,
			cache: 'false',
			success: function(data){
				console.log(data)
				if(data == true){
					$("#alert_listName").show();
					$("#btnAddShoppingList").prop('disabled',true);
				}else{
					$("#alert_listName").hide();
					$("#btnAddShoppingList").prop('disabled',false);
					statusName = true;
				}
			}
		});
	}

	var x = 0;
	
	for (i = 1; i <= 13; i++) { 
		$(".floor-icon" + i).on("click", function(){
			var id = $(this).attr('href');
	 		var offsets = $(id).position();
	 		var top = offsets.top - 110;
	 		var retrievedObject = localStorage.getItem('objHref');
	 		if(retrievedObject == null){
	 			localStorage.setItem('objHref', id);
	 			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: top }, "slow");
	 		}else{
	 			if(id != retrievedObject){
	 				$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: top }, "slow");
	 				localStorage.setItem('objHref', id);
	 			}else{
	 				return false;
	 			}
	 		}
		});
	}

	function fetchJSONFile(path, callback) {
	    var httpRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
	    httpRequest.onreadystatechange = function() {
	        if (httpRequest.readyState === 4) {
	            if (httpRequest.status === 200) {
	                var data = JSON.parse(httpRequest.responseText);
	                if (callback) callback(data);
	            }
	        }
	    };
	    httpRequest.open('GET', path);
	    httpRequest.send(); 
	};
	
	fetchJSONFile('/getFloors', function(data){
	    window.floorJSON = data;
	});

	$('.tab-selector').hover(function() {
		f = $(this).attr('href').replace('#', '').split('-');
		if (curFloor[f[0]] != f[1]) {
			$('a[href="#' + f[0] + '-0"]').removeClass('active');
			loadFloorItem(f[0], f[1], this);
		}
		curFloor[f[0]] = f[1];
		
		if (f[1] == 0) {
			$('#slide-tab-'+f[0]+' .active').attr('class', '');
			$('a[href="#' + f[0] + '-' + f[1] + '"]').addClass('active');
			pushGAFloorProduct(this);
		}
	});
	
	function loadFloorItem(catId, subcatId, element) {
		var hero = [];
		try {
			for(i = 0; i < floorJSON.length; i++) {
				if(floorJSON[i].categoryId == catId) {
					if (subcatId == 0) {
						if(floorJSON[i].heroProducts.length > 0)					
							hero = floorJSON[i].heroProducts;
						
						break;
					} else {
						for(j = 0; j < floorJSON[i].childs.length; j++) {
							if(floorJSON[i].childs[j].categoryId == subcatId) {
								hero = floorJSON[i].childs[j].heroProducts;
								break;
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		} catch (e) {
		}
		
		var h = 0;
		for(; h < Math.min(hero.length, 8); h++) {
			var visHide = '';
			curDiv = '#hero-' + catId + '-' + (h+1);
			$(curDiv).css('visibility','visible');
			
			// link
			$(curDiv + ' .link').attr('href', hero[h].url);
			$(curDiv + ' .link img').attr('src', hero[h].image).attr('alt', hero[h].name);
			
			// caption
			$(curDiv + ' .caption a').attr('href', hero[h].url);
			$(curDiv + ' .caption a').text(productSubstring(hero[h].name, 32));
			
			// price
			dStart = new Date(hero[h].special_date_start);
			dEnd = new Date(hero[h].special_date_end);
// 			if(curDate > dStart && curDate < dEnd) {
// 				if($(curDiv + ' .col-xs-8 p.fprice').length == 0) {
// 					$(curDiv + ' .col-xs-8').html('<p class="fprice">Rp ' + currencyFormat(hero[h].price) + '</p><p class="lead">Rp ' + currencyFormat(hero[h].special_price) + '</p>')
// 				}
// 			} else {
// 				$(curDiv + ' .col-xs-8').html('<p class="lead">Rp ' + currencyFormat(hero[h].price) + '</p>')
// 			}
			if(curDate > dStart && curDate < dEnd) {
				if($(curDiv + ' .col-xs-8 p.fprice').length == 0) {
					visHide = '';
				}
			} else {
				visHide = 'style="visibility:hidden"';
			}
			
			if(hero[h].price == hero[h].special_price){
				visHide = 'style="visibility:hidden"';
			}
			
			$(curDiv + ' .col-xs-8').html('<p class="fprice" ' + visHide + '>Rp ' + currencyFormat(hero[h].price) + '</p><p class="lead">Rp ' + currencyFormat(hero[h].special_price) + '</p>')
			
			// discount
			$(curDiv + ' .col-xs-4').html('<span class="discount-tag" style="visibility:hidden">-' + hero[h].discount_percent + '%&nbsp;</span>')
			if(curDate > dStart && curDate < dEnd) {
				if(hero[h].discount_percent > 0){
					$(curDiv + ' .col-xs-4').html('<span class="discount-tag">-' + hero[h].discount_percent + '%&nbsp;</span>')
				}
			}
			
			if (f[1] != 0) {
				$(curDiv + ' .link img').removeClass('ga-view-floor-product');
				
				if ($(element).attr('flag') == 0) {
					gap.pushProductImpression2(hero[h], 'Homepage - Floor Product', h+1);
				}
			} else if (f[1] == 0) {
				$(curDiv + ' .link img').addClass('ga-view-floor-product');
			}
			
			$(curDiv + ' .link').attr('onclick', 'pushGAProductClick2(' + catId + ', ' + subcatId + ', ' + h + ')');
			$(curDiv + ' .caption a').attr('onclick', 'pushGAProductClick2(' + catId + ', ' + subcatId + ', ' + h + ')');
			
		}
		for(; h < 8; h++) {
			curDiv = '#hero-' + catId + '-' + (h+1);
			$(curDiv).css('visibility','hidden');
		}
		
		if (f[1] != 0) {
			if ($(element).attr('flag') == 0) {
				$(element).attr('flag', 1);
			}
		}
	};
	
	function productSubstring(arg1, arg2){
		var str = arg1;
		var lStr = str.length;
		
		if(lStr > arg2){
			str = str.substring(0, arg2);
			var arr = str.split(" ");
			var strArr = "";
			for(var i = 0; i < arr.length - 1; i++){
				strArr += arr[i];
				if(i < arr.length - 2)
					strArr += " ";
			}
			str = strArr + "...";
		}
		
		return str;
	}
	
});

	function pushGAProductClick2(catId, subcatId, index) {
		var obj = [];
		try {
			for(i = 0; i < floorJSON.length; i++) {
				if(floorJSON[i].categoryId == catId) {
					if (subcatId == 0) {
						if(floorJSON[i].heroProducts.length > 0)					
							obj = floorJSON[i].heroProducts;
						break;
					} else {
						for(j = 0; j < floorJSON[i].childs.length; j++) {
							if(floorJSON[i].childs[j].categoryId == subcatId) {
								obj = floorJSON[i].childs[j].heroProducts;
								break;
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		} catch (e) {
		}
		
		gap.pushProductClick2(obj[index], "Homepage - Floor Product", index+1);
	}
}

	}

<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
	jQuery.validator.addMethod("emailvalid", function(sEmail) {
		var filter = /^([\w-\.]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
		return filter.test(sEmail);
	}, "Please enter a valid email address.");
	
	$('#subscribeNewsletter').validate({
		errorClass: 'error-subscribe',
		focusInvalid: false,
		ignore: "",
		rules: {
			email: {
				required: true,
				email: true,
				emailvalid: true
			}
		},
		highlight: function(element) {
	        $(element).parent('div').addClass('has-error');
	    },
	    unhighlight: function(element) {
	        $(element).parent('div').removeClass('has-error');
	    },
	    errorPlacement: function(error, element) {
			if (element.attr("name") == "email" )
				error.insertAfter(".error-subscribe");
			else
				error.insertAfter(element);
		}
	});
});
</script>
